Sjith awoth hodai‚ù§
Me welawe kalabala wenna hoda na. Ranil gemak gahanna yanne. Malimawe kattiya molen gema gahanna ona. Kalabala athi kaloth ranil, onna jvp karayo mehemai kiyla pennai. Hamoma kalabala nowee.molen wadak karamu.anura kiyna deta sawan demu.
